 Why is the last day of Chhath so important? - On the last day of Chhath, Sun is offered to Arun Vela - This arghya is given to "usha", the wife of Surya - This Chhath festival ends with the offering of Arghya
 After this arghya, women open the fast by drinking water and eating prasad - Chhath festival and every day has its own different significance, only by giving the last arghya of Chhath is fulfilled
 lekin sabase zyada myne rakhata he chhath vrath kaa samaapan

 *** Nirmal Verma was a real world writer
 ek ghumkkad or shabd sandhan ke maahir
 Written and praised in every genre of prose
 upanyaas, kahaniyaan, yatra-vrutant, lekh, naatak, sansmaran, patr aadi
 He was born on April 3, 1929 in Shimla
 unke lekhkeey kaushal ko isi se samaj sakate hai ki unki darjanon kitaaben unke jeevankaal main to chhapi hin, ab bhi chap rahi hai
 He was awarded all the best honors of literature
 inamen sahitya academy puraskaar, gyanpith puraskaar, sahitya academy mahattar sadsyta ullekhneey hai
 He was also awarded the Padma Bhushan, the third highest civilian honor by the President of India
 kaha jaataa he ki bharat sarkaar ne nirmal verma ko aupchaarik rup se nobel puraskaar ke liye namit kiya tha
 Today, on his birth anniversary, we are giving a part of his essay compilation 'shabd aur Smriti' published by Vani Prakashan for the readers of 'sahitya Aaj Tak'
 is sangrah ke bare main khud nirmal verma ne likhaa tha- roman khandhiron yaa puraane muslim makbaron ke bich ghoomte hue ek ajeeb gahari udaasi ghir aati he jaise koi hitchkee, koi saans, koi chikh inke bich fansi rah gayi ho
 
 
 Who neither can get rid of the past, nor can get passion in the present
 
 
 kintu yah udaasi unke liye nahin he, jo ek ja-maane main jivit the or ab nahin hai
 
 
 He has a lot to himself, who will not survive to see the ruins one day
 
 
 puraane smarak or khandhar hamen us mrityu kaa bodh karaate hai, jo ham apane bheetar lekar chalate hai, bahata pani us jivan kaa bodh karaata he, jo mrityu ke baavjood vartmaan he, gatisheel he, antahin he
 
 
 In 'word and Smriti', Nirmal Verma made it clear that the question is not of 'indian experience', but of Indian 'smriti' and that 'smriti' is born of a distinct connection between the person and the past, a cultural connection ', Therefore, the question of memory is not of history, but of 'culture'
 prastut he nirmal verma ke 'shabd or smriti' niabandh sangrah kaa ek adhyay xxrep 6 * 'srijan-prakriya or moolyankan'ek kalakaar-mere liye hameshaa ek bohemian or vidooshak rahaa he, isliye jo lekhak apane ko bahut gambheertha se lete hai, ve hameshaa mujhe kuch haasyaaspad-se jaan padate rahe hai
 Actually, the art of every art lies in a satire - as much towards society, as towards ourselves
 ek buddhijivi aalochak gambheer hota he ki aksar kala main khel or vyangy kaa tatva hameshaa uski aankhon se ojhal ho jaataa he
 Perhaps this is why, whenever i have had the opportunity to write about the author's creation process, there is a strange sense of insignificance - as much as towards ourselves, towards his words
 jaahir he, is chote-se lekh se main us nirarthakta ko or aage badha rahaa hoon, lekin us dukhad ahsaas ke baavjood main is prakriya ke kuch naye pahaluon ko dekh paane kaa lobh sanvaran nahin kar paata
 The difficulty is that seeing - as we commonly use this word - is almost impossible for the creation-process
 ek pathak yaa darshak kii vaastavik zindagi kis seemaa par, kis khaas bindu par lekhak kii anubhoot vaastaviktaa ko chhu sakegi, uske marm ko bhed sakegi, yah nirnay karnaa kaafii kathin he
 Regarding this, no critic - no matter how sensitive he is - could not determine any kind of rule
 koi bhi kalakriti apane anubhav kii prakriya main sampoorn he, vah apni hi sharton par aadhaarit he
 Once born, the perceived reality has no relation to the reality from which it draws inspiration, but does not live or live on it
 vaastaviktaa kaa anubhav hameshaa usase alag rahegaa, jo vaastavik he
 What is real is the average life of daily activities, no matter how intense it is in itself, it will inevitably break after going beyond one breath
 alag-alag ausat ghatnaon ke bich us zindagi ko pakad paanaa, jo dainik jivan ke vikrut samjhauton, uske thande hote hue nirnyon ke baahar he (uske bich hote hue bhi)
 This is what a writer can do to dare to transcend daily reality, to project his perceived reality on the screen of real reality
 marxvaadi aalochak george lukach kaa yah kathan apane main bahut mahatvapurn he ki anna carinina sahi rup main usee kshan jivit ho paati he, jahaan vah aatmahatya karne ke liye tatpar hoti he
 
 
 Because at that moment, Tolstoy puts her in an extreme situation, where other women who are dissatisfied with their husbands live only by compromise
 har mahatvapurn lekhak kaa anubhav charam sthiti kaa anubhav he, jahaan vah dainik jivan ke yatharth ko peeche chhod jaataa he
 
 
 In the process of being left behind, he frees his heart from the darkness of average reality
 ek lekhak ke liye yah vikat sthiti he-ek had tak dukhad bhi
 The real life which is necessary for creation is always outside of it, it cannot be consumed freely, because the process of enjoyment is self-destructive to all those elements which are essential for creation
 jis tarah ek pathak srijan-prakriya ke baahar he, keval uske taiyaar maal ke sampark main aa paata he, usee tarah ek kalakaar vaastavik zindagi ke baahar he- yaa us zindagi ke baahar he, jise ham vaastavik maanate hai or vah aakhir tak is pidaa-yukt antarvavandv main fasaa rahata he ki baahar rahakar vah kahin us asaliyat ko to nahin kho rahaa jo sirf bhogane par hi apni ho paati he
 We will let this 'subtle' deliberation of critics remain separate, wherein they describe the 'enjoyment' of the artist as different and higher than the level of 'enjoyment' of an ordinary person
 
 
 kam-se-kam kalakaar ko apane vyaktigat jivan main isse koi santvana nahin mil sakati
 To experience and experience - these two are completely different things - no artist knows it as much as any other person knows it
 ek ‘academik', yaa academy kaa 'lekhak' to shaayad kabhi is antar ko mahasoos hi nahin kar saktaa
 
 
 He is free from outside risk
 kuch din pehle vaan gogg ke patron ko padhate sahasaa meri ankhen in vaakyon par atak gayi thim
 Writing to his brother Theo, he thinks: i have always felt that at the root of everything lies the life of ordinary people
 kabhi-kabhi mujhe yah vichaar kaafii dukh detaa he ki ham vaastavik zindagi main nahin hai
 
 
 i mean that it is better to work in blood and plaster than to work in blood and plaster, to give birth to children, or to get into a business, is much more pleasant than making pictures
 lekin iske baavjood jab main yah sochataa hai ki meri hi tarah mere kai dost vaastavik zindagi ke baahar hai to main phir se apane ko jivit mahasoos karne lagata hai
 At a glance, even when we live outside this real life, we still find ourselves connected to it in a cursed form
 vah hamen akelaa karti he lekin apane main akelaa nahin rahane detii
 Many people feel lonely in the crowd
 
 
 usamen koi anokhi baat nahin, lekin apane akelepan main bheed ke dabaav ko mahasoos karnaa
 
 
 Even if you do not compromise with him, you can hear the scratching of his fingernails on his door - this can only be relieved by the writer who frees himself from the destiny of the artist
